                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.3"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dviyoniścaturvikalpobhihitaḥ snehaḥ snehaguṇāś ca | tatra jaṅgamebhyo
                        gavyaṃ snehaṃ pradhāṇatamaṃ sthāvarebhyas tilasneha iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ yathāprayojanato yathāpradhānataś ca | sthāvarasnehāṃ vakṣyāmaḥ
                        | tatra
                        tilvakairaṇḍakuśāmradantīpalāśaśaṅkhinīviṣāṇigavākṣīkampilyakaśampākanīlinīsnehā
                        virecayanti |. jīmūtakakūṭajakṛtavedhanekṣvākumadanasnehā vāmayanti |.
                        viḍaṅgasthū lamañjarīmadhuśigrusūryavallīpīlusiddhārthakajyotiṣmatīsnehāḥ
                        śiro virecayanti | karañjapūtīkalavaṇamātuluṅgeṅgudīkirātatiktakasnehāḥ
                        duṣṭavraṇeṣūpayojyāḥ |. turuvakakapitthabhallātakapaṭolasnehāḥ mahāvyādhiṣu
                        |. trapusatvārukerkāratumvurukaṣmāṇḍasnehāḥ mūtrasaṅgeṣu
                        ||kapotavaṅkaharītakīsnehāḥ śarkarārśmariṣu |.
                        kusumbhasarṣapātasīpicumardātimuktakakāṇḍīrasnehāḥ prameheṣu |.
                        nāḍīkerapanasapiyālavilvamadhūka śleeṣmātakasnehāḥ pittasaṃsṛṣṭe vāyau ||
                        vibhītakapiṇḍītakabhallātakasnehāḥ kṛṣṇīkaraṇeṣu |. śravaṇakaṃgukasnehāḥ
                        pāṇḍūkaraneṣu | saralāpītadāruśiṃśapāsanasārasnehāḥ dardrukiṭibheṣu | sarva
                        eva snehā vātam upahanti | tailaguṇāḥ samāsena vyākhyātāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.6">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ kaṣāyapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra kecidāhus tvak
                        patrapuṣpaphalādīnāṃ bhāgastaccaturguṇamudakaṃ caturthāṃśāvaśeṣitaṃ
                        kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ | tat tu na samyak kasmād
                        āgamasiddhatvāt </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.7">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         palakuḍavādīnām ity etac copadekṣyāmaḥ | tatra dvādaśadhānyamāṣā madhyamā
                        suvarṇṇamāṣakaste śoḍaṣasuvarṇṇāḥ | ataścordhvaṃ caturguṇamabhivardhayataḥ
                        palakuḍavaprasthāḍhakadroṇā abhiniṣpadyante | tulā punaḥ palaśataṃ tābhir
                        viṃśatir bhāraḥ śuṣkāṇām ārdrāṇāṃ dravāṇāṃ ca dviguṇam iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.8">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehakukuḍavesāṇyakvāthyadravyadurvyaprastho vidheyas taccaturguṇamudakaṃ
                        caturthāṅgāvaśeṣitaṃ kvāthyāvatārayed ity eṣa kaṣāyakalpaḥ |
                        snehakuḍavesāṇya bheṣajapalaṃ kalkam iṣṭaṃ caturguṇañ ca kaṣāyam āvāpya
                        vipaced ity eṣa snehapākakalpa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.9">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.10">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.11">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrdhvaṃ snehapākakramam upadekṣyāmaḥ | sa tu pākas tṛvidho
                        mṛduścikkanaḥ kharacikkaṇa iti | dhavivekamātraṃ yatra bheṣajaṃ sa mṛduḥ |
                        madhūcchiṣṭamivalepayati yatra bheṣajaṃ sa cikkaṇaḥ | phenāni mātra vailasya
                        śeṣaṃ ghṛtavadādiśet kṛṣṇamavasannamīṣadviśadaṃ cikkaṇaṃ ca yatra sa
                        kharacikkaṇa iti |. ata ūrdhvaṃ pradagdhasneha bhavati | taṃ punaḥ sādhayet
                        | tatra pānābhya va nasyābhyañjanīyaś cikkaṇaḥ | vastisnehāḥ kharacikkaṇa
                        iti ||</l>

                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         siddhametad ghṛtaṃ pītaṃ sadyasnehanamucyate |.
                        <caesura/>
                         nṛpāṇāṃ tat samānānāṃ deyametad ghṛtottamaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.45">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         balahīneṣu vṛddheṣu mṛdvagnistrī mahātmani |
                        <caesura/>
                         alpadoṣeṣu yojyā syu ye yogāḥ samyagīritāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.46">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vivarjayet snehapānamajīrṇṇī taruṇajvarī |
                        <caesura/>
                         durvalārocakī sthūlo mūrcchārtto madapīḍitaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.47">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         chardyābhibhūtastṛṣitaḥ śrāntaḥ pānaklamānvitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vastidatto viriktaś ca vānto yaś cāpi mānavaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.48ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.48cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.48cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         akāle ca prasūtā strī snehapānaṃ vivarjayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.49">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehapānād bhaved nṝṇāṃ nānāvidhā gadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gadā vā kṛcchratāṃ yānti na sidhyantyatra vā yataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.50"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.51ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.51cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.51cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaṃ purīśaṃ grathitaṃ bhuktaṃ kṛcchreṇa pacyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.52ab"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.52cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.52cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         durvarṇṇo durbalaś caiva rūkṣo bhavati mānavaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.53">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         glāniḥ sadanamaṅgānām adhastāt snehadarśanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak snigdhasya liṅgāni snehodvegas tathaiva ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.54">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhaktadveṣo mukhāsrāvo gudadāha pravāhikā |
                        <caesura/>
                         purīśātipravṛttiś ca tadatisnigdhalakṣaṇaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.55">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣasya snehanaṃ snehairatisnigdhasya rūkṣaṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śyāmākakoradūṣānnatakrapiṇyākaśaktubhiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.56">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.56</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dīptāntaragniḥ pariśuddhakoṣṭhaḥ pratyagradhāturbalavarṇṇayuktaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛḍhendriyo mandarajāḥ śatāyuḥ snehopasevī puruṣo bhaved hi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.31.57">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.31.57</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sneho hito durbalavahnidehesandhukṣaṇe vyādhinipīḍitasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         valānvito bhojanadoṣajātaiḥ pramardituṃ tau sahasā na śakyāviti ||</l>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">

                    <head>[Adhyāya 32]</head>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svedāvacāraṇīyaṃ cikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra caturvidhaḥ svedā bhavati |. tad yathā tāpasvedo bāṣpasvedaḥ
                        |upanāhasvedo dravasvedaś ceti | tatra svedavikalpāvarodhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tāpasvedo nāmapālikāṃ sakandaphalavāṃlikāvastraiḥ prayujyate
                        śayānasya bāṣpatāpoṅgāraiḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bāṣpasvedas tu kapālapāṣāṇoṣṭakalohapiṇḍān agnivarṇān adbhir
                        āsicyatairārdravastrapariveṣṭitaiḥ | svedayed aṅgapradeśā evaṃ
                        māṃsarasapayodadhisnehadhānyāmvlavātaharapatrabhaṃgakvāthapūrṇṇam vā kumbhīm
                        abhiprataptāṃ prāvṛtyoṣmāṇaṃ gṛhṇīyāt | pārśvacchidreṇa vā kumbhena tasyāḥ
                        kumbhyāmukhena mukhamabhis andhāya tasminañchidrehastiśuṇḍākāraṃ nāḍīṃ
                        praṇidhāya śayānaṃ svedayet</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.6">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhopaviṣṭaṃ svabhyaktaṃ prāvṛtam vā |. bha ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hastiśuṇḍikayā nāḍyā svedayed vātarogiṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhaṃ sarvānugā hyeṣā na ca saṃkleṣayen naraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.7">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāmārdhamātratrivakrahastihastasamākṛtiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedanārthe hitā nāḍī kailiñjī hastiśuṇḍikā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8ab">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.8ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣāyāmamātram vā bhūmim utkīrya khādiraiḥ </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.8cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.8cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāṣṭair avadāhyābhyukṣya vātahara</l>

                    <l met="hypermetrical" xml:id="SS.4.32.9">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.9" met="hypermetrical</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         patrabhaṅgairavacchādya śayānaṃ svedayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         śilātalamavadāhyāpohya bhasmaṃ ca pūrvavat |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.10">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuṭīm vā caturdvārāṃ kṛtvā tasyām upaviṣṭasyāntaś caturvāṃgārān
                        anuparidhāya svedayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.11">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāśadhānyāni vā samyagusvedyāstīrya kiliñjenyasmiṃ vā tatpratirūpake
                        śayānaṃ svedayed evaṃ pāṃśu gośakṛttuṣapa lāloṣmabhiḥ svedayed iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.12">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upanāhasvedas tu vātaharadravyakalkair amvlapiṣṭair lavaṇapragāḍhaiḥ
                        susnigdhaiḥ sukhoṣṇaiś ca pradihya svedayed evaṃ kākolyādirelāsu rasādim
                        āhṛtya tilātasīsarṣapakalkair vā kṛsaraveśavārapāyasotkārikābhir vā etābhir
                        eva vāyo dūlikāṃ vadhvā svedayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.13">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravasvedas tu vātaharadravyakvāthapūrṇṇakoṣṭakaṭāhe droṇyām vāvagāhya
                        svedayet | evaṃ payomāṃsarasayūṣatailaghṛtadhānyāmvlamūtreṣvetair eva
                        sukhoṣṇaiḥ pariṣiñcediti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.14">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tāpoṣmāsvede viśeṣataḥ śleṣmaghnau | upanāhasvedo vātaghnaḥ |
                        anyatarasmiṃ pittasaṃsṛṣṭadravasveda iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.16">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         caturvidho yo 'bhihito dvādhā svedaḥ prayujyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         svasminn eva dehe tu dehasyāvayave tathā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.17">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yeṣān nasyaṃ vidhātavyaṃ bastiś cāpi hi dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śodhanīyāś ca ye kecit pūrvaṃ svedyās tu me matāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.18">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         paś cāt svedyāhṛte śalye mūḍhagarbhānupadravā |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak prajātā kāle ca paś cāt svedyaiva jānatāṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.19">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pūrvāṃ svedyā paś cāc ca bhagandaryarśaśas tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmaryāṃ cāturo jantu śeṣāñcāstre pravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.20">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nānabhyakte nāpi cā snigdhadehe yojyaḥ svedyaḥ svedavidbhiḥ kathañcit |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛṣṭaṃ loke kāṣṭham asnigdhamāśur yāyāt bhaṅgaṃ svedayogair gṛhītaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.21">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedaklinnā dhātusaṃsthā tu doṣāḥ svasthānasthā ye ca mārgeṣu līnāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyak svedair yojitais te dravatvaṃ prāptāḥ koṣṭhaṃ śodhanair yātyaśeṣāḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.22">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         agne dīptin mārdavaṃ tvakprasādaṃ bhaktaśraddhāṃ srotasāṃ nirmalatvaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kuryāt svedas tandrīnidre ca hanyāt | sandhīm katvāṃśceṣṭayed āśuyuktaḥ
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.23">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svedāsrāvo vyādhihānirlaghutvaṃ śītārthitvaṃ mārdavaṃ cāturasya |
                        <caesura/>
                         samyaksvinne lakṣaṇaṃ prāhuretat | mithyāsvinne viparītaṃ tad eva ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.24">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sphoṭotpattiḥ pittaraktaprakopo madāmūrcchābhramadāho klamaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         atisvinne sandhipīḍā ca tṛṭca śītā kriyās tatra kuryād vidhijñaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.25">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍumehī raktapittī tṛṣārttaḥ kṣutakṣīṇo durvalo jīrṇṇabhaktaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dakodarīgarbhiṇī pānapañca naite svedyā yaścamartyotisārī |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedād eṣā yāṃti dehāvināśaṃ asādhyatvaṃ yānti caiṣāṃ vikārāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         svedaiḥ sādhyo durvalojīrṇṇabhaktā yadi syātāṃ svedanīyau tatastau |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.26"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.27">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvasvedāṃ nivāte tu jīrṇṇānne cāvacārayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehābhyaktaśarīrasya śītair ācchādya cakṣuṣī |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.28">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atisvinnam athāsvābhya śītāṃbutrāsanaṃ hitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snānam uṣṇāmbunā caiva nivatañcālayayet |</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.32.29cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.32.29cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhojayec cānabhiṣyandi sarvaṃ vācāram ādiśed iti ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">ci|| ❈||</p>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 33]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanavirecanasādhyopakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ calitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ pravṛddhā nirhattavyāḥ
                        svasthānasthārakṣyā iti siddhāntaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prādhānyena vamanavirecanenirharaṇe varttate | tasmāt tayor vidhānam
                        ucyamānam upadhārayasva |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathāturaṃ snigdhasvinnam anabhiṣyandibhir āhārair anavabaddhadoṣam
                        ālocya svo vamanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti saṃbhojayet | saṃbhojyas tu tīkṣṇāgnir
                        balavān bahudoṣo mahāvyādhiparigṛhīto vamanasātmyaś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         peśalair vividhairannair doṣamutkliśya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnāya vamanaṃ dattaṃ samyak pravarttate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāparedyuḥ pūrvāhṇe sādhāraṇe kāle
                        vamanadravyakaṣāyakalkacūrṇṇasnehanānyatamasya mātrāṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        asātmyabībhatsadudarśanadurgandhāni vāmanīyāni vidadhyād ato viparītāni |.
                        tatra sukumārāṃ kṛśaṃ bālaṃ vṛddhāṃ bhīrum vā vamanasādhyavikāreṣu
                        kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭhaṃ pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        pītauṣadhañcapāṇibhir agnitaptair upaspṛśyamānaṃ muhūrttam upekṣeta | tatra
                        pravṛttahṛllāsaṃ jñātvā jānumātrāsanopaviṣṭam anyena hṛtpṛṣṭhayoḥ pāṇibhyāṃ
                        uparigṛhītam aṅguligandharvahastapatravṛttotpalanālānām anyatamena
                        kaṇṭhamanabhis pṛśan vāmayet yāvat samyag vāntalakṣaṇāni bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.8">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaprasekaṃ hṛdayāviśuddhiṃ kaṇḍūñ ca duścharditaliṅgam āhuḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittātiyogañ ca visaṅjñatāñ ca hṛtkaṇṭhapīḍām api cātivānte |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.9">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte kaphasyāndramukhaṃ pravṛtte śuddheṣu hṛtkaṇṭhaśirassu cāpi |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghau ca dehe kaphasaṃsrave ca sthite suvāntaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.10">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         samyagvāntaṃ cainam abhis amīkṣya snaihikavairecanikopaśamanīyānāṃ dhūmānām
                        anyataṃ sāmarthyataḥ pāyayitvā cārikam upadiśet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.11">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tato parāhṇe suvibhaktadeham uṣṇābhir ahniḥ pariṣiktagātraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kulattham udgaḍhakijāṅgalānāṃ yuṣai rasair vāpy upabhojayīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.12">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaprasekaḥ svarabhedatandrā nidrāsyadaurgandhyaviṣopasargāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurutvakaṇḍūgrahaṇīpradoṣā na santijantorvamataḥ kadācit |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.13">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         chinne tarau puṣpaphalaprarohā yathāvināśaṃ sahasā vrajanti |
                        <caesura/>
                         tathāhṛte śleṣmaṇi ccharddanena tajjā vikārā vilayaṃ vrajanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.14">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na vāmayet taimirikannagulminaṃ na caivapāṇḍūdararogapīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthūlakṣatakṣīṇakṛśātivṛddhā narśorditā kṣepakapīḍitāṃś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.15">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaṃ pramehe taraṇe ca garbhe gacchatyadhordhvaṃ rudhire ca tīvre |
                        <caesura/>
                         tuṣṭe ca koṣṭhe krimibhir manuṣyaṃ na vāmayed varcasi cātivṛddhe ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.17">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ete py ajīrṇṇavyathitā vāmyā ye ca viṣāturāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         atīvacolbaṇakaphās te ca syur madhukāmbunā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.19">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanam api snigdhasvinnāya ca deyaṃ | avāntasya hi samyagviriktasyāpi
                        satovasrastaḥ śleṣmāgra haṇīñ chādayati | gauravam āpādayati pravāhikām vā
                        kurute | tasmāt snigdhasvinnāya vāntāya ca deyam |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.20">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāturaṃ svo virecanaṃ pāyayitāsmīti pūrvāhṇe laghubhojayet |
                        phalāmvlamuṣṇodakaścainamanupāyayet | athāparehani vigataśleṣmadhātāvāt
                        uropakramaṇīyād apekṣyāturam athāsmai virecanaṃ mātrāṃ prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.21">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra mṛduḥ krūro madhya iti trividhaḥ koṣṭho bhavati | tatra bahupitto
                        mṛduḥ sa dugdhenā viricyate | bahuvātaśleṣmā krūro durvirecyaḥ | sagadoṣo
                        madhyaḥ sādhāraṇa iti | tatra mṛdau mṛdvī mātrā | tīkṣṇakrūre | madhye
                        madhyā karttavyeti | pītauṣadhaś ca tanmanāḥ śayyābhyāse viricyeta | na
                        prāptavegaṃ vidhārayet | na cāprāptaṃ prāṇenākāṃkṣeta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.22"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.23">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā ca vamane krameṇa prasekauṣadhaḥ pittānilāgacchanty evaṃ virecane
                        vātamūtrapurīṣapittakaphā iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.24">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bha ||hṛtkukṣyaśuddhiḥ paridāhakaṇḍūviṇmūtrasaṃgaś ca na sadvirikte |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāgudabhraṃśakaphātiyogāḥ śūlodgamāś cātiviriktaliṅgaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.25">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gateṣu doṣeṣu kaphāntakeṣu glānyelaghutve manasaś ca tuṣṭau |
                        <caesura/>
                         gatenile cāpy anulomabhāvaṃ samyagviriktaṃ puruṣaṃ vyavasyet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.26">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mandāgnimakṣīṇamasadviriktaṃ na pāyayet tad divasaṃ yavāgūṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇaṃ tṛṣārttaṃ suvirecitaś ca tanvī sukhoṣṇaṃ laghu pāyayīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.27">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         buddheḥ prasādaṃ balamindriyāṇāṃ dhātusthiratvaṃ jvalanābhivṛddhiṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         cirāc ca pākaṃ vayasaḥ karoti virecanaṃ samyagupāsyamānaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.28">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathodakānāṃ tu vijaṅgamānāṃ rodhevadīrṇṇe dhruva eva nāśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte hṛtendhevam upadravāṇāṃ pittātmikākānāṃ vihito vināśaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.29">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣīṇāḥkṛśārūkṣitabālavṛddhādīnotha śoṣī bhayaśokataptaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śāntas tṛṣārtto parijīrṇṇabhakto garbhiṇyadho gacchati yasya cāsṛk |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.30">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         navapratiśyāyaparītadeho navajvarīyā ca navaprasūtā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyan ity āna virecanīyā snehādibhir ye tv anupaskṛtāś ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.31">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyarthapittābhiparītadehāṃ virecayet tān api mandamandaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanair yāṃti narā vināśam ajñaprayuktair avirecanīyā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.32"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.33">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.34">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.35">

                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdukoṣṭhasya dīptāgner dattaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na samyag nirhared doṣān ativegapradhāvitaṃ |</l>

                    <l met="hypermetrical" xml:id="SS.4.33.36">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.36" met="hypermetrical</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prātar yad auṣadhaṃ pītaṃ bhaktapākasame kṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         paktaṃ gacchati doṣāṃs tu nirharen niravaśeṣataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.37">

                        <caesura/>
                         durbalasya naḥ punaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         haret prabhūtānalpāṃs tu samayet pracyutānatha |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.38">

                         hareddoṣāṃ calān pakvaṃ balino durbalasya vā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.39">

                        <caesura/>
                         sandhukṣitāgni snigdhañ ca svinnañcaiva viśodhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.40">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.41">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.33.41</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.42"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.43">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.44">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.45">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.33.46">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanavirekavyāpaccikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyāturanimittam vamanam virecanañ ca || pañcadaśadhā vyāpadyate tatra
                        vamanasyādho gacchaty ūrddhvam virecanasya | sāmānyam ubhayoḥ
                        sāvaśeṣauṣadhatvam alpadoṣahṛtatvaṃ jīrṇṇauṣadham vātaśūlam ayogātiyogau
                        jīvādānamādhmānam parikarttaḥ parisrāvaḥ pravāhikā hṛdayasaraṇa vibandha iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra bubhukṣāpīḍitasya tīkṣṇāgner mmṛdukoṣṭhasya vāvatiṣṭhamānaṃ
                        durvvāntasya vā guṇasāmānyād vamanam adho gacchati | tatrepsitān avāptir
                        ddoṣo kleśaś ca tam āśusnehayitvā bhūyastīkṣṇatarair vvāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apariśuddhāmāśayasyotkliṣṭaśleṣmaṇaḥ sāvaśeṣān nasya vā'hṛdyam
                        bahudhāvacāritam vā virecanam ūrddham tiṣṭhati tatrepsitān avāptibastidoṣān
                        kleśatamulbaṇaśleṣmāṇamāśu || 1|| vāmayitvā bhūyas tīkṣṇatarair vvirecayet
                        iti | āmāśaye tvāmavat samvidhānaṃ | ahṛdyetiprabhūte ca hṛdyam
                        pramāṇayuktañ ca | tathā tathāpy uttiṣṭhati tṛtīye nna pāyayet ataś cainam
                        madhughṛtaphāṇitayuktairllehayitvā virecayet iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.6">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣavigrathitamalpamauṣadham avasthitamūrddhabhāgikam adhobhāgikam vā na
                        sraṃsayatidoṣān | tatra
                        tṛṣṇāpārśvaśūlañccharddimūrcchāparvvabhedohṛllāsorucirudgarāviśuddhiś ca
                        bhavati | tam uṣṇābhir adbhir āśu vāmayet | ūrddhvabhāgikam adhobhāgikam vā
                        sāvaśeṣauṣadham apradhāvitadoṣam atibalamasamyag viriktalakṣaṇam upayuktam
                        alpam apy evam vāmayet iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.7">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krūrakoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇāgner alpamapyauṣadham alpaguṇam vā bhaktavat pākam
                        upaiti | tatra samudīrṇṇa doṣāḥ | yathākālam anirhriyamāṇā vibhramaṃ
                        kurvvanti | tamanalpamamandañcauṣadham pāyayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.8">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnenālpam alpaguṇam vā bheṣajam upayuktam alpān doṣān harati |
                        taddoṣaśeṣam vamanagauravam upakleśa hṛdayāṃ viśuddhiṃ vyādhivivṛddhiñ ca
                        karoti roga)| tatra yathāyogam pāyayitvā vāmayed dṛḍhataraṃ |
                        virecanadoṣaśeṣaṃ gudaparikarttam ādhmānaṃ gauravamanisaraṇam vāyor
                        vvyādhivivṛddhiñ ca karoti | tam upapādya snehasvedābhyāṃ bhūyo virecayed
                        dṛḍhataraṃ | dṛḍhaṃ pracalitadoṣam vā tṛtīye divasa iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.9">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         asnigdhasvinne rūkṣamauṣadham upayuktamabrahmacāriṇā vā vāyuṃ kopayati |
                        tatra vāyuḥ prakupitaḥ pārśvapṛṣṭhaśoṇitamanyāmarmma muśūlaṃ mūrcchā bhrama
                        saṃjñānāśañ ca karoti | tadvātaśūlam ity ācakṣate | tamabhyajya
                        dhānyasvedena svedayitvā yaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena tailenānu vā vāmayed iti
                        pāṭhaḥ |sayati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.10">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehasvedābhyām avibhāvita śarīreṇauṣadhamalpaguṇam vā pītamūrddhamadho vā
                        nābhyeti doṣām̐ścopakleśya taiḥ saha balakṣayamāpādayati | tatrādhmānaṃ
                        hṛdayagrahastṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaś ca bhavati | tam ayogam ity ācakṣate |tam āśu
                        vāmayed virecayed vā durvvāntasya tu samutkliṣṭā doṣāḥ | vyāpyaśarīraṃ
                        kaṇḍūśvayathukoṭhapiṭakajvarāṅgasādanāni kurvvanti tatas tān aśeṣān
                        sahauṣadhenāpaharet | durvviriktasya tu stabdhapūrṇṇodaratā
                        bastiśūlomeḍhratodo vātamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaśaḥ kaṇḍūrmaṇḍalaprādurbbhāvaś ca
                        bhavati | tamāsthapya punaḥ snehayitvā virecayet tīkṣṇeneti |
                        nātipravarttamāne tiṣṭhati vā duṣṭasaṃśodhane tatsantejanārtham uṣṇodakam
                        pāyayet | pāṇitāpaiś ca pārśvodaram upasvedayet tataḥ pravarttate doṣāḥ |
                        anupravṛtte 'lpe doṣe jīrṇṇecauṣadhe ca bahudoṣam antaḥ śailam balañ
                        cāvekṣya bhūyo mātrāṃ<del>ñ ca</del> vidadhyād anupravṛtta bhenyūbhaṃ vā
                        daśajātrādūrddham upasthitadehaṃ bhūyaḥ śodhayed durvviriktamāsthāpya punaḥ
                        snehayitvā virecayet | hrībhayalobhaiś ca vegāghātaśīlāḥ prāyaśaḥstriyo
                        rājasamīpasthā vaṇijaḥ śrotriyāś ca bhavanti | tasmād etair ddurvvirecyāḥ |
                        bahuvātatvāt | ataścaināṃ susvinnasnigdhān virecayed iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.11">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhasvinnasyātimātramatimṛdukoṣṭhasyātitīkṣṇamadhikam vābheṣajamatiyogaṅ
                        kuryāt | tatra vamanātiyoge pittātipravṛttir bbalavisraṃso vātakopo
                        balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajyāvagāhya ca śītā svapsu śītaiḥ
                        śarkkarāmiśrair llehair upacared iti | virecanātiyoge
                        kaphātipravṛttiruttarakālañ ca saraktasya tatrāpi balavisraṃsā vātakopo
                        balavām̐ś ca bhavati | tamabhyajya śītābhir adbhiḥ pariṣicyāvagāhya śītais
                        taṇḍulāmbubhir mmadhumiśrair vvāmayet | picchābastiñcāsmai dadyāt |
                        kṣīrarasayoścainam anyatamena bhojayet kṣīrasarppiṣā cainam anuvāsayet |
                        priyaṅgvādiñcāsmai taṇḍulāmbunā pātum prayacchet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.12">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmin eva ca vamanotiyoge tipravṛtte śoṇitaṃ ṣṭhīvati ccharddayati vā
                        raktaṃ tatra jihvāniḥsaraṇam avasarppaṇañ cākṣṇor vvyāvṛttihanusaṃhananaṃ
                        tṛṣṇā hikkāṅgarau visaṃ jñatvam ity upadravā bhavanti | tam
                        ativisrutaśoṇitavidhānena nopacaret |
                        jihvānniḥsarppitāntrikaṭukalavaṇacūrṇṇapraghṛṣṭāmantaḥ pīḍayet praviṣṭāyām
                        anyemlamasya purastāt khādeyuḥ | vyāvṛtte cākṣiṇī ghṛtābhyaktaiḥ pīḍayet |
                        hanusaṃhanane vātaśleṣmaharan nasyaṃ svedañ ca vidadhyāt | tṛṣṇādiṣu ca
                        yathāsvaṃ pratikurvvīta | visaṃjñam vā veṇuvīṇāgītasv enaṃ srāvayed iti
                        |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.13">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanātiyoge sacandrakaṃsalilam adhaḥ sravati tato
                        māṃsadhāvanaprakāśamuttarakālaṃ jīvaśoṇitañ ca | tatra gudaniḥsaraṇaṃ
                        vepathur vvamanātiyogopadravāś ca bhavanti | tam atisrutavidhānenaivopacaret
                        | niḥsarppitaṅ gudam abhyajya parisvedyān pīḍayet | kṣudrarogacikitsite
                        gudasraṃsacikitsitañ cāvekṣyeta | vepathau vātavyādhividhānaṅ kurvvīta |
                        jihvāniḥsarppaṇādiṣūktaḥ pratīkāraḥ | atipravṛtte vā nyagrodhādikaṣā
                        yakṣīrekṣurasaghṛtasaṃsṛṣṭaiś cainaṃ bastir upācaret | śoṇitaniṣṭhīvane
                        raktātisāraraktapittakriyāś cānyasya vidadhyān nyagrodhādiñ cāsya
                        pānabhojaneṣūpayuñjīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.14">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīvaśoṇitaraktapittayo jijñāsārtham picu plotam vātra prakṣipet tad
                        uṣṇodakaprakṣālitam avarajyeta taj jīvaśoṇita m ity avagantavyam amṛgbhoktum
                        vā śune dadyāt sa yady upayuñjyāt taj jīvaśoṇitam ity avagantavyam iti |
                        tayoś ca raktipittātīsārakriyām vidadhīta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.15">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sa śeṣānnenānilaprāyakoṣṭhenāsnigdhena vā pītamauṣadham ādhmāpayati |
                        tatrānilamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaḥ | samunnaddhodaratā pārśvabhaṅgo gudabastitudanañ
                        ca bhavati | tamādhmānam ity ācakṣate | tam upasvedyānāha
                        varttidīpanabastikriyābhir yojyā iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.16">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṣāmeṇātimṛdukoṣṭhena tīkṣṇamatyuṣṇam atilavaṇ atirūkṣam vā bheṣajam
                        upayuktam pittānilau pradūṣya nātibastigudaparikarttanam āpādayati | tām
                        parikarttiketyācakṣate || taṃ yaṣṭīmadhukakṛṣṇatilamadhughṛtayuktaiḥ
                        picchābastibhir āsthāpayet | śītāmbupariṣiktañcainaṃ payasā bhuktavantaṃ
                        ghṛtam aṇḍanayaṣṭīmadhukasiddhena vā tailenānuvāsayed iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.17">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         krūrakoṣṭhasyātiprabhūtadoṣasya vā mṛdvalpamauṣadhamavacāritaṃ samutkleśya
                        doṣānna niḥśeṣān apaharati | pākañcopaiti | tatra
                        daurbbalyodaraviṣṭambhārucirggātrasadanāni bhavanti | sa vedanau
                        cāsyapittaśleṣmāṇau sravatas tam parisrāvam iti ācakṣate |
                        tamajakarṇṇadhavatiniśa palāsakaṣāyair mmadhuyuktair āsthāpayet |
                        upaśāntadoṣam bhūyaḥ saṃśodhayed</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.18">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atirūkṣetisnigdhe vā bheṣajam avacāritam aprāptaṃ purīṣam udīrayato
                        vigevighātena pravāhikā bhavati | tatra sadāha śūlaṃ svetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ raktam vā
                        bhṛśaṃ pravāhamāṇaḥ kapham upaviśati | tam pratisrāvavidhānenopacaret</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.19">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yast ūrddhvam adho vā bheṣajaṃ vegapravṛttam ajñānād vinihanti
                        tasyopasaraṇaṃ hṛdi kurvvanti doṣas tatra pradhānamarmmasantāpād vedanābhir
                        atyartham pīḍyamādantāṃ kaṭakaṭāyatyudvṛttākṣo jihvāṃ khādati
                        pratāmyamānacetā ca bhavati | tam abhyajya dhānasvedena svedayitvā tīkṣṇena
                        dviśiro virecanenopacared yaṣṭīmadhukamiśreṇa cainan taṇḍulāmbunā vāmayed
                        yathā doṣaguṇocchreyaś cainam bastibhir upācared iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.20">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yas tūrddhvam adho vā pravṛttadoṣaḥ śītāṅgāram udakam anilam anyad vā
                        seveta tasya doṣāḥ srotaḥsv avalīyamānā ghanībhāvam āpannā
                        vātamūtrapurīṣagraham āpādya vibadhyante || tasyāṭopo jvaro dāho vedanā ca
                        tīvrā bhavati | tam āśu vāmayitvā prāptayitvā prāptakālaṃ kriyāṃ yojayed iti
                        || adho bhāge tv abhāgaharadravye saindhavāmlalavaṇa mūtrasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ pāyayed
                        āsthāpanam anuvāsanañ ca yathādoṣam vidadhyād yathādoṣam āhārakramaś ca |
                        ūrddhvabhāge tu upadravaviśeṣāt yathāsvaṃ pratikurvvīta |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.21">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yā tu virecane gudaparikīrttitā tad vamāne kañcakaṣaṇaṃ yadadhaḥ
                        parisravaṇaṃ sa ūrddhaṅ kaphaprasekaḥ | yā tvadhaḥ pravāhikā sa ūrddhaṅ
                        śuṣkoṅkādgāra iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.22">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.34.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yās tv etā vyāpadaḥ proktā daśapañca ca tatvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         etā virekāti yogā duryogā yogajāḥ smṛtāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.34.trailer">|| cikitsā lahya ||</l>
                </div>


                <div n="35" type="adhyāya">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         || athāto neetrabastipramāṇavibhāgacikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atra snehādīnāṅkarmmaṇām bastikarmmapradhānatamam ācakṣate | kasmād
                        anekakarmmaprakāratvāt | ba stirihakhalu nānāvidhadravyasaṃyogād doṣāṇāṃ
                        saṃśodhanaṃ saṃśamanasaṅgrahaṇāni karoti | kṣīṇam vyājīkaroti | kṛśaṃ
                        bṛṃhayati | sthūlaṃ karṣayati | cakṣuḥ prīṇayati | balīpalitam upahanti |
                        vayaḥ sthāpayati iti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīropacayaṃ varṇṇabalamārogyamāyuṣaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         parivṛddhiñ ca karoti basti samyagupāsitāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā jvarātīsāratimirapratiśyāyaśirorogādhimanthārdditā
                        kṣepakāghātaikāṅgasarvvāṅgarogādhmānodaraśūlavṛddhyupadaṃśānāhamūtrakṛcchragulmavātaśoṇitavātamūtrapurīṣasaṅgaśukrodāvarttaśukrārttabas
                        tanyanāśahṛddhanumanyāgrahaṇaśarkkarāśmarimūḍhagarbbhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vikāreṣv
                        atyartham upayujyata iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.6">

                        <caesura/>
                         bastirvvāte ca pitte ca kaphe rakte ca pūryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃsargge sannipāte ca bastir eva sadā hitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.7">

                        <caesura/>

                        kanīnikānāmikāmadhyamāṅgulipariṇāhāni
                        agreṅgulādhyarddhāṅguladhyarddhāṅgulatryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇṇikāni
                            śyenabarhikaṅka<del>gṛdhra</del>patranāḍītulya praveśānāni mudgamāṣaka
                        lāyamātrāsrotāṃsi vidadhyān netrāṇīti | teṣu cāsthāpanadravyapramāṇam
                        āturahastasammitausanmiśrau prasṛtau dvau catvārāṣṭau vidheyā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.8">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.9">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.9</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        agre tryaṅgulasanniviṣṭakarṇṇikaṃ gṛdhra patranāḍītulyapraveśaṃ
                        kolāsthimātraṃ cchidraṃ klinnakalāyamātracchidram ity eke ||
                        āsthāpanamātrapramāṇaṃ dvādaśaprasṛtā iti | saptasaptyānyās tu
                        ūrddhannetrapramāṇam etad eva | āsthāpanamātrāpramāṇan tu dviraṣṭavarṣavad
                        iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.10">

                        <caesura/>
                         mṛdurbbastiprayoktavyā viśeṣād bālavṛddhayoḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tayostīkṣṇaḥ prayuktas tu bastihiṃsyādbalaujasī ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.11">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.12">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.12</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        dṛḍhāni gopucchākṛtīni | guṭikāmukhāni ceti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.13">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.35.13</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        mahiṣagovarāhāḍorabhrāṇāmanyatamam āsādyeti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.35.14">

                        <caesura/>

                        ityanarthāntaraṃ | tasya vikalpo mādhutailikaḥ | tasya paryāyaśabdo
                        yuktarathaḥ siddhabastiriti | sarvvadoṣanirharaṇāccharīrarohaṇādvā nirūhaḥ
                        sthāpanādāyuḥ sthānād vā āsthāpana iti | paś cāt mādhutailikavikalpān
                        upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra yathā pramāṇaguṇavihitaḥ snehabastiḥ pādāpakṛṣṭaḥ |
                        snehabasti vikalporddhamātrāpakṛṣṭonuvāsanaḥ| anavasannapi na duṣyata
                        ityanudivasam vā dīyata ityanuvāsanaḥ | tasyātivikalpo '
                        rddharthamātrāpakṛṣṭo 'pahāryo mātrābastiriti ||</l>

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">Adhyāya 36 (draft based on MS H)</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto netrabastivyāpaccikitsitam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.2.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.2.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra netrañ calitam vivarttitam pārśvāvapīḍitam atyuttkṣiptam avasannan
                        tiryakkṣiptam iti ṣaghraṇidhānadoṣāḥ | atisthūlaṅ karkkaśāgram avanatam
                        anubhinnasannikṛṣṭakarṇṇikaṃ śūkṣmātimajacchidram alpam atidīrgham
                        atihrasvam ity ekādaśanetradoṣāḥ || bahalatālpatā cchidratā prastdhānatā
                        durbbaladurbbaddheti tveti pañca bastidoṣāḥ | atipīḍitatā śithilapīḍitatā
                        bhūyo vapīḍitatā kālātikramateti catvāraḥ pīḍanadoṣāḥ | āmaṃ hīnam atimātram
                        atiśītam atyuṣṇam atitīkṣṇaṇ ativṛddham atisnigdham atirūkṣm atisāndram
                        atidravam ity ekādaśadravyadoṣāḥ | avāṅcīrṣo cchīrṣony
                        ubjauttānasaṅkucitotthitasatthitādadakṣiṇapārśvaśāyinam avanatapratānam ity
                        aṣṭau śayyādoṣāḥ | evam etāḥ pañcacatvāriṃśad vyāpado vaidyanimattā bhavanti
                        |āturanimittās tu pañcadaśa āturopadravīye vakṣyante | snehastvaṣṭābhiḥ
                        kāraṇaiḥ praṇihito na pratyāgacchati | tad yathā tribhir doṣai
                        rasanābhibhūto malavyāmiśro dūrānupraviṣṭo svinnasyānuṣṇolpaṃ bhuktavato
                        lpāṃśaś cetyetāḥ | vaidyāturanimittā bhavanti | ubhayor bbastyor ayogaḥ |
                        ādhmānaṃ parikarttaḥ parisrāvaḥpravāhikā hṛdayopasaraṇam aṅgapragraho tiyogo
                        jīvādānam ity etān avavyāpado vaidyanimittā eva bhavanti || ṣaṭsaptabhiḥ
                        samāsena vyāpadaḥ parikīrttitāḥ |tāsāṃ vakṣyāmi vijñānaṃ siddhiñ ca
                        tadanantaraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.3">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.24">

                         tatrottaro hito basti susvinnasya sukhāvahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyubjasya bastir nāpnoti pakvādhāṇaṃ virnirgataḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.25">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdgude bādhate cātra vāyuḥ pṛṣṭham athāpi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttānasyāvṛte mārge bastiḥ prastheti dehinaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.26">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kuñcitaḥ sakthadehasya yat kamayam asaṃprāpya |
                        <caesura/>
                         bastir nivartate kṛcchrād anya tatra niyojayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.27cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.27cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sthitasya bastir dattas tu kṣipram āyāty avāṅmukhaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.28">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāśayaṃ tarpayati tasmānnārthakaro mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāpnotibastir dattas tu kṛtsnaṃ pakvāśayaṃ punaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.29">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dakṣiṇāśritapārśvasya vāmapārśvānugo hi saḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nyubjādīnāṃ yathādānaṃ tadvadbastir na śasyate ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.30">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yaś cāpy anilakopo tra yathāsvaṃ tatra siddhayaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehabastinimittās tu vakṣyante vyāpadaḥ purā |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.31">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehabastividhāv eva salakṣaṇacikitsitāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anuṣṇolpauṣadhī hīno bastir nneti prayojitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.32">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.32</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣṭambhādhmānaśūlaiś ca tam ayogam pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tīkṣṇo hito bastis tīkṣṇañ cāpi virecanaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.33">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.33</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtadoṣapramāṇena saṃsarggaś ca vidhīyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         atyāsitañ cātibahur bbastir mmandoṣṇa eva ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.34ab"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.34cd">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.34cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā bahupurīśañ ca kṣipram ādhmāpayen naraṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.35">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.35</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛtkaṭīpṛṣṭhapārśveṣu śūlās tatrātidāruṇāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra tīkṣṇataro bastir hitañ cāpy anuvāsanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.36">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.36</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atitīkṣṇoṣṇalavaṇo rūkṣo bastiḥ prayojitaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sapittaṃ kopayed vāyuṅ kuryāt saparikarttikān |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.37">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nābhibastir ggudan tatra kṛtyanta iti dehinaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra snehaś ca madhuraiḥ śritaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.38">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.38</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyuṣṇatīkṣṇalavaṇaḥ parisrāvāya kalpate |
                        <caesura/>
                         daurbbalyam aṅgasādañ ca jāyate tatra dehinaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.39">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.39</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         parisravatyadhaḥ pittaṃ dāhaḥ sañjanayed gude ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra bastiḥ kṣīraghṛtasya ca |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.40">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.40</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pravāhikā bhavettīkṣṇā nirūhāt sānuvāsanāt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sadāhaśūlaṃṃ kṛcchreṇa kaphantatropaveśyate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.41">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.41</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastir hitas tatra payasā caiva bhojanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarppir madhukasiddhañ ca tailam vāpy anuvāsanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.42">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.42</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atitīkṣṇo nirūho vā satatam vānuvāsanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdayasyopasaraṇaṃ kurute 'thāṅgasādanaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.43">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.43</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣais tatra rujāstīvrā mado mūrcchāṃ sagauravaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvadoṣaharaṃ bastiṃ śodhanaṃ tatra dāpayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.44">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.44</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣasya bahuvātasya syād duḥkhaṃ śayitasya vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bastipragraham aṅgānāṃ kuryād rukṣo lpabheṣajāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.45">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.45</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrāṅgasādaprastambha jṛmbhodveṣṭanavepakāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvabhedaś ca tatreṣṭāḥ svedābhyañjanabastayaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.46">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.46</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atyuṣṇatīkṣṇo 'tibahur ddattātisveditasya vā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         alpadoṣasya vā bastir atiyogāya kalpate |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.47">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.47</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         virecanātiyogena samānan tatra lakṣaṇaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         picchābastiḥ samābhyāsa<del>ḥ</del>s tasya śītaḥ sukhāvahaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.48">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.48</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atiyogāt paraṃ hanti jīvādānam viriktavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         dehaṃ deyāṃs tatra hitānāhuḥ picchābastiṃ saśoṇitaṃ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.49"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.50"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.36.51">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.36.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pakṣād vireko vāntasya nirūhahyaś cānuvāsitaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sadyo niruho 'nuvāsasya saptarātrād virecita iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.3">

                         virecanāt saptarātre gate jātabalāya vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtāhārāya sā yāhne bastir ddeyo nuvāsanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.4">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.5">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.6">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.46">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.47">

                         rātrau bastir nna dadyāc ca doṣotkleśo hi rātrijaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.48">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.49">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.37.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte 'dhike kaphe kṣīṇe rūkṣe vātarujārdite |

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.50">

                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇe pittedhikevāpi divādāhādayo gadāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sambhavanti tadā stvenam pradoṣe yojayed bhiṣak ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.51"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.52">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.53">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.54">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.55">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.56">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.57">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.57.1">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.57.2">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.58">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.59">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.76">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.77">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.37.77</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehabastin nirūham vā nābhyased eka eva tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehātpittakaphotkleśo nirūhāt pavanādbhayaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.37.78">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto nirūhakramacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38a">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarirddharmmabhṛtām variṣṭham amṛtodbhavaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraṇāvupasaṃṅgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38b">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38b</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagavaṃ snehavastes tu tathaivāsthāpanasya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         pramāṇaṅkalpanaṅ kālam mātrāñ cāpi bravīhi me ||
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38c">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38c</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuddhe muhūrtte karaṇe dine ca nakṣatrayoge ca tathānukūle |
                        <caesura/>
                         viviktasaṃsṛṣṭamṛdāvalipte vicitrapuṣpāstṛtabhūpradeśe ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38d">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38d</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇṇarūpyāya satāmrajo vā mṛdūdbhavo vā kalaśo 'mbupūrṇṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sadhānyaratnādi samālyagandhair vastrādibhiś cāpy atha svastikaiś ca ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38e">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38e</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         taccāmṛtasthānam ato 'rccanīyaṃ pūrvvāt tatonyaddhṛṣayaḥ sadevāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃspṛśya ratnāni tathauṣadhīm̐ś ca devān dvijān pūjya ca dakṣiṇābhiḥ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38f">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38f</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         tanmadhya saṃsthāyabhiṣak prasanna iti pāṭhaḥ |bhiṣag apramattaḥ sunirmmale
                        syāt sudṛḍho viśāle ||
                        <caesura/>
                         suvarṇṇalohādi mṛdūdbhavo vā pragṛhyakāṃse 'py atha rājate vā ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38g">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38i">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38k">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āturam anuvāsitam āsthāpayet | svabhyaktaṃ svinnaśarīram utsṛṣṭa
                        bahirbbhāgamapravāte śucau deśe samavinyastāyāṃ śayyāyām adhaḥ |
                        sapratigrahāyām āśroṇīpradeśe suvyūhāyāṃ śayānam vāmapārśve neti || bhavati
                        cātra ślokaḥ || savyam prasārayet sakthi dakṣiṇaṃ cāpasaṃharet | madhyāhne
                        sumanājīrṇṇe niranno vāgyatonaraḥyataḥ || tato vāmapādopari netraṃ
                        kṛtvetarapādāṅguṣṭhāṅgulībhyāṅ karṇṇikopari nipīḍya bastāv
                        auṣadhamāsicyocchrāsyauṣadhānte cāvavadhya mūtreṇa samyag baddhañ cāturā ya
                        ghṛtābhyaktanetrāgraṃ ghṛtābhyakta gudāya praṇayed anutsṛjannanupṛṣṭhavaṃśam
                        anusukham ākarṇṇikam iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.4">

                        <caesura/>
                         ekenaiva ca pīḍena na drutan na vilambitaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.5">

                         tato netram apanīya triṃśan mātrāpīḍanakālād upetyottiṣṭhetyāturam brūyāt |
                        utkuṭukobhavatasterāgamanāyeti |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.6">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.7">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.38.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         api hīnaṃ kramaṅ kuryān na ca kuryād atikramaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣāt sukumārāṇāṃ hīna eva kramo hitaḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         alpālpavego vinvāta hīnohīno nirūhaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.38.8.1">

                         yavakolakulatthānāṃ kvātho māgadhikāyutaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sasaindhavaḥ samadhukaḥ siddhabastir iti smṛtaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.1">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.4">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.39.5">

                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 40]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.1">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dhūmanastaḥ kavalacikitsitaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.3">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcavidho dhūmo bhavati | tad yathā | prāyogikaḥ snaihiko vairecanikaḥ
                        kāsaghno vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.4">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrailādinā kuṣṭhatagaravarjyena ślakṣṇapiṣṭena dvādaśāṅgulaṃ śarakāṇḍaṃ
                        daśāṅgulagarbham aṅgula m aṅguṣṭhodara pariṇāhaṃ kṣaumeṇāṣṭāṅgulam
                        pariveṣṭyālepayed eṣā varttiḥ prāyogikaḥ ||
                        snehaphalasāramadhūcchiṣṭasarjarasagugguluprabhṛtibhiś ca snehamiśraiḥ
                        snaihikaiḥ || śirovirecanadravyair vairecanikaiḥ ||
                        bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikātrikaṭukakāsamardahiṃgviṅgudītvaṅmanaḥśilācchinnaruhākarkaṭakasṛṅgīprabhṛtibhiḥ
                        kāsaharaiḥ kāsaghnaiḥ |
                        snāyucarmakhuraśṛṅgakarkaṭāsthiśuṣkamatsyavallūrakrimibhir vāmanīyaiś ca
                        vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.5">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra bastinetravyavyair dūmanetradravyāni vyākhyātāni bhavanti ||
                        dhūmanetraṃ tu kanīnikāpariṇāham agre kalāyamātrasroto mūle ṅguṣṭhapariṇāhaṃ
                        dhūmavarttipraveśasroto ṅgulāni catuścatvāriṃśat prāyogike | dvātriṃśat
                        snaihike | caturviṃśati vairecanike | ṣoḍaśakāsaghne | daśa vāmanīya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.6">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha sukhopaviṣṭaḥ sumanā ṛjvadhodṛṣṭir atandritaḥ | snehapradīptāgrām
                        varttinetrasrotasi praṇidhāya dhūmam pibed iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.7">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhena tam pibet pūrvaṃ nāsikābhyān tataḥ pibet |
                        <caesura/>
                         mukhapītaṃ mukhenaiva vamet pītañ ca nas tataḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.8">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo vamen nastato dhūman nastapītaṃ mukhena vā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa netrakarṇṇanāsāsyasaṃśrayāl labhate gadān || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.9">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu prāyogikaṃ ghrāṇenādadyāt | snaihikaṃ mukhanāsābhyāṃ |
                        nāsikābhyāṃ vairecanikaṃ | mukhenaivetarāv iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.11">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        śramabhayāmarṣoṣṇaviṣaraktapittamadamūrcchāpipāsātāluśoṣamūrdhābhighātodgāratimiramehodarādhmānordhvavātontravṛddhibālavṛddhadurbalaviraktāsthāpitajāgaritagarbhiṇīrūkṣakṣatakṣīṇoraskāḥ
                        madhughṛtadadhidugdhamadyayavāgūpītāḥ svalpakaphāś ca dhūman na severann iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.12">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         akālapīto bhramarī śirorogaṃ karoti ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāsrotokṣijihvānāṃm upaghātañ ca dāruṇaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.13">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmaḥ snaihiko vairecanikaḥ prāyogiko dvādaśasu kāleṣūpayogo bhavati ||
                        tad yathā
                        kṣutadantaprakṣālananasyasnānabhojanādivāsvapnamaithunacchardanamūtroccārābhir
                        uṣitaśastrakarmānteṣv iti || tasya vibhāgo
                        mūtroccārakṣavathuruṣitamaithunānteṣu snaihikaḥ | divāsvapnacchardanāntayor
                        vairecanikaḥ | dantaprakṣālanasya snānabhojanaśastrakarmānteṣu prāyogika iti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.14">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra snaihiko vātaṃ śamayati | snehād upalepitvāc ca | vairecanikaḥ
                        śleṣmāṇam utkliśyāpakarṣati raukṣyāt taikṣṇyād auṣṇyād vaiṣadyāc ca |
                        prāyogikaḥ śleṣmāṇam utkleśayaty utkliṣṭaṃ cāpakarṣayati śamayati vā
                        sādhāraṇatvāt pūrvābhyām iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.15">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmaprayogāt puruṣaḥ prasannendriyavāṅmanā |
                        <caesura/>
                         dṛḍhakeśadvijaḥ śmaśrusugandhiviśadānanaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.16">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tathā
                        kāsaśvāsārocakāsyapralepasvarabhedamukhāsrāvakṣavathuvamathukrāthatandrīhanumanyāstambhapīnasaśirorogalocanaśūlāvātakaphanimittāś
                        cāsya mukharogā na bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.17">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya yogāyogātiyogā vijñātavyā bhavanti | yogas tu dṛṣṭaphalārthaḥ | ayogo
                        rogānirjayaḥ | atiyogas
                        tāluśoṣaparidāhapipāsābhramamadamūrcchākarṇṇakṣveladṛṣṭirogādaurbalyayutam
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.18">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra prāyogikas trīṃs trīn ucchvāsān ādadyāt paryāgatāns trīns trīṃś
                        caturo veti || snaihikaṃ yāvad asrupravṛttiḥ || vairecanikam ādoṣadarśanāt
                        || grāsāntareṣu kāsaharaṃ || vairecanikavat tilataṇḍulayavāgūpīto vāmanīyaṃ
                        yathāyoga iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.19">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vraṇabastinetreṇa vraṇadhūmanetraṃ vyākhyātam bhavati ||
                        <caesura/>
                         śarāvasampuṭayutaṃ vraṇadhūman nayed vraṇaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhūmanetreṇa matimān vedanāsrāvaśāntaye ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.20">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhir eṣa samāsena dhūmasyābhihito mayā ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nasyasyātaḥ pravakṣyāmi vidhiṃ kuśalasammitaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.21">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         auṣadhapakvo vā sneho nāsikābhyāṃ pradīyate | nasyan tatpañcavikalpam
                        bhavati | tad yathā | nasyaṃ śirovirecanaṃ pratimarśo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanam
                        iti | teṣān nasyam pradhāṇaṃ śirovirecanaṃ yena nasya vikalpaḥ pratimarśaḥ |
                        śirovirecanavikalpo vapīḍaḥ pradhamanañ ceti | tato nastaśabdaḥ pañcavidhā
                        ṇipatati | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.22">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yaḥ snehārthaṃ śūnyaśirasāṃ grīvāskandhorasāṃ balajananārthaṃ
                        dṛṣṭiprasādajananārtham vā sneha upādīyate tasmin vaiśeṣike nastaśabdaḥ |
                        tat tu deyam vātābhipanne śirasi tathā
                        dantakeśaśmasruṇātadāruṇakarṇṇakṣvelatimirasvaropaghātanāsārogamukharogaśoṣāvabāhukākālajavalīpalitaprabodheṣu
                        vātapaittikeṣu ca mukharogeṣu vātapittaharadravyasiddhena sneheneti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.23">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śirovirecanam api śleṣmaṇābhivyāptatālugataśirasāṃ tathā
                        rocakaśirogauravaśūlapīnasāvabhedakakrimipratiśyāyāpasmāraghrāṇājñāneṣv
                        anyeṣu cordhvajatrugateṣu vikāreṣu śirovirecanadravyasiddhena sneheneti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.24">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tv etad dvividham apy uktaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.25">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatroccāritavātamūtrapurīṣāya bhuktavate vyabhre kāle
                        pāṇitāpopasveditagalakapolalalāṭapradeśāya vātātaparajohīne veśmany
                        uttānaśāyine kiñcit pravilambitaśirase vastrāvacchāditanetrāya
                        vāmahastapradeśinyagronnāmitanāsāgrāya viśuddhasrotase dakṣiṇahastena śuktyā
                        picunā vā sukhoṣṇam adrutam avicchinnadhārām āsiñced iti | yathā ca netreṇa
                        prāpnoti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.26">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snehe vasicyati śiro na kathañ cana kampayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         na bhāṣen na ca kupyec ca na kṣuyān na hased api | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.27">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.27</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etair hi vihataḥ sneho na samyak pratipadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tataḥ kāsaḥ pratiśyāyaḥ śirokṣigadasambhavaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.28">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya pramāṇan tv aṣṭau bindavaḥ pradeśinīparvadvayaniḥsrutāḥ | eṣā mātrā
                        prathamā | dvitīyā śuktiḥ tṛtīyā pāṇiśuktir ity etās tisro mānāḥ yathābalam
                        prayojyā bhavantīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.29"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.30">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śṛṅgāṭakam abhiplāvya nireti vadanād yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphotkleśabhayāccainan niṣṭhīved avidhārayan || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.31">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.31</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dante punar api saṃsvedya galakapolādīn dhūmam āseveta | bhojayec cainam
                        anabhiṣyanti | athāsyācārikam upadiśet | krodhādim pariharec ca |
                        rajodhūmamanastāpadravapānaśirasnānādīni | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.32">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         vikāropaśamaḥ śuddhir indriyāṇām paraṃ sukhaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.34">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.34</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ayoge rogānirjayaḥ kaphaprasekaḥ śiraso gurutendriyavibhramaḥ | k> atiyoge
                        tāluśoṣapipāsābhramamadamūrcchā ceti lakṣaṇam mūrdhny atisnigdhe rūkṣaṃ
                        tatrāvacārayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.35"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.36">

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.37">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.37</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya trīṇy abhivarṇṇyante lakṣaṇāni prayogataḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.38">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.38</label>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.39">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.41">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.42">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.51">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.51</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratimarśes tu caturdaśasu kāleṣūpadeyo bhavati | tad yathā | kālyotthitena
                        | prakṣālitadantena | gṛhān nirgacchatā | vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrātena |
                        mūtroccārakavalāñjanān te bhuktavatā | charditavatā | divāsvapnotthitena
                        sāyañ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.52">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.52</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kālyotthitenāsevitaḥ pratimarśo rātrāv upacitaṃ nāsāsrotogataṃ malam
                        apahanti | prakṣālitadantena dantānāṃ dṛḍhatā vadanasaugandhyañ cāpādayati |
                        gṛhān nirgacchatā nāsāsrotaso snehaklinnatayā | rajodhūmo vā na prabādhate |
                        vyāyāmavyavāyapariśrāntena śramam apahanti | mūtroccārānte dṛṣṭigurutvam
                        apanayati | kavalāñjanānte dṛṣṭiṃ prasādayati | bhuktavatā sroto viśuddhiṃ
                        laghutvaṃ cāpādayati | charditavatā srotovilagnaṃ śleṣmāṇam apohya
                        bhaktacchaṃdaṃ kurute | divāsvapnotthitena nidrāśeṣaṃ gauravañ cāpahatya
                        cittaikāgryaṃ janayati | sāyaṃ sukhanidrāprabodham āpādayatīti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.53">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.53</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         īṣad ucchiṃghaṇāt sneho yadā vaktum prapadyate |
                        <caesura/>
                         naste niśiktaṃ taṃ vidyāt pratimarśaṃ pramāṇataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.4.40.54">
                        <label>1938 ed., 4.40.54</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
